# Metasibir Avatar Creator - AGENTS.md

## Purpose
- New project root for building an independent avatar creator.
- This file contains full source dataset for the selected 441 Ready Player Me assets.

## Dataset Scope
- Extracted for subdomain: demo
- Filters: bodyType = generic + fullbody, gender = male + neutral
- Included asset types: top, bottom, footwear, outfit, hair, eye, glasses, headwear, beard, facewear
- Total assets: 441

## Type Counts
- beard: 36
- bottom: 28
- eye: 19
- facewear: 12
- footwear: 20
- glasses: 63
- hair: 94
- headwear: 38
- outfit: 98
- top: 33
